## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend)

### 1. Auctions Data
- Path: data/auctions.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields Order and Names:
  1. auction_id (int)
  2. item_name (str)
  3. description (str)
  4. category (str)
  5. starting_bid (float)
  6. current_bid (float)
  7. end_time (str, format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
  8. status (str: Active, Closed, Upcoming)
  9. image_url (str)
- Purpose: Stores details of all auctions including current bids and statuses.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|Vintage Leather Watch|Antique leather wristwatch from the 1950s|Collectibles|25.00|45.50|2025-02-15 18:00|Active|watch.jpg
  2|iPhone 14 Pro|Latest Apple smartphone in excellent condition|Electronics|500.00|620.00|2025-02-10 12:00|Active|iphone.jpg
  3|Wooden Desk|Beautiful oak wood desk with original finish|Furniture|75.00|110.00|2025-02-08 20:00|Closed|desk.jpg
  ```

### 2. Categories Data
- Path: data/categories.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields Order and Names:
  1. category_id (int)
  2. category_name (str)
  3. description (str)
  4. item_count (int)
- Purpose: Stores category information for filtering and display.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|Electronics|Digital devices and gadgets|15
  2|Collectibles|Rare and valuable collector items|28
  3|Furniture|Household furniture and decor|12
  ```

### 3. Bids Data
- Path: data/bids.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields Order and Names:
  1. bid_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. bidder_name (str)
  4. bid_amount (float)
  5. bid_timestamp (str, format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
- Purpose: Records all individual bids placed on auctions.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|45.50|2025-02-05 14:30
  2|2|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45
  3|3|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-04 10:15
  ```

### 4. Winners Data
- Path: data/winners.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields Order and Names:
  1. winner_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. item_name (str)
  4. winner_name (str)
  5. winning_bid (float)
  6. win_date (str, format: YYYY-MM-DD)
- Purpose: Stores information about auction winners and winning bids.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08
  2|5|Victorian Mirror|Diana Prince|95.00|2025-02-03
  3|7|Vintage Books Set|Eve Stewart|150.00|2025-02-01
  ```

### 5. Bid History Data
- Path: data/bid_history.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields Order and Names:
  1. history_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. auction_name (str)
  4. bidder_name (str)
  5. bid_amount (float)
  6. bid_timestamp (str, format: YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
- Purpose: Logs detailed bid history for auctions.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Alice Johnson|40.00|2025-02-05 13:00
  2|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Frank Miller|42.50|2025-02-05 13:45
  3|2|iPhone 14 Pro|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45
  ```

### 6. Items Data
- Path: data/items.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields Order and Names:
  1. item_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. item_name (str)
  4. starting_price (float)
  5. category (str)
  6. condition (str)
  7. seller_name (str)
- Purpose: Stores item details including conditions and sellers.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|25.00|Collectibles|Excellent|John Collector
  2|2|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Like New|Tech Store
  3|3|Wooden Desk|75.00|Furniture|Good|Antique Shop
  ```

### 7. Trending Data
- Path: data/trending.txt
- File Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields Order and Names:
  1. auction_id (int)
  2. item_name (str)
  3. bid_count (int)
  4. current_bid (float)
  5. trending_rank (int)
  6. time_period (str)
- Purpose: Stores ranked trending auction data for different time ranges.
- Example Rows:
  ```
  2|iPhone 14 Pro|12|620.00|1|This Week
  1|Vintage Leather Watch|8|45.50|2|This Week
  5|Vintage Camera|6|85.00|3|This Week
  ```

---

End of Design Specification Document


=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
import os

app = Flask(__name__)
app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'

DATA_DIR = 'data'

# Helper functions for reading and writing data

def read_auctions():
    auctions = []
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
            for line in file:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 9:
                    auction = {
                        'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'item_name': parts[1],
                        'description': parts[2],
                        'category': parts[3],
                        'starting_bid': float(parts[4]),
                        'current_bid': float(parts[5]),
                        'end_time': parts[6],
                        'status': parts[7],
                        'image_url': parts[8]
                    }
                    auctions.append(auction)
    return auctions


def write_auctions(auctions):
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt')
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as file:
        for a in auctions:
            line = '|'.join([
                str(a['auction_id']),
                a['item_name'],
                a['description'],
                a['category'],
                f"{a['starting_bid']:.2f}",
                f"{a['current_bid']:.2f}",
                a['end_time'],
                a['status'],
                a['image_url']
            ])
            file.write(line + '\n')


def read_categories():
    categories = []
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'categories.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
            for line in file:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 4:
                    category = {
                        'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'category_name': parts[1],
                        'description': parts[2],
                        'item_count': int(parts[3])
                    }
                    categories.append(category)
    return categories


def read_bids():
    bids = []
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
            for line in file:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 5:
                    bid = {
                        'bid_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                        'bidder_name': parts[2],
                        'bid_amount': float(parts[3]),
                        'bid_timestamp': parts[4]
                    }
                    bids.append(bid)
    return bids


def write_bids(bids):
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt')
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as file:
        for b in bids:
            line = '|'.join([
                str(b['bid_id']),
                str(b['auction_id']),
                b['bidder_name'],
                f"{b['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                b['bid_timestamp']
            ])
            file.write(line + '\n')


def read_winners():
    winners = []
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'winners.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
            for line in file:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 6:
                    winner = {
                        'winner_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                        'item_name': parts[2],
                        'winner_name': parts[3],
                        'winning_bid': float(parts[4]),
                        'win_date': parts[5]
                    }
                    winners.append(winner)
    return winners


def read_bid_history():
    bid_history = []
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
            for line in file:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 6:
                    history = {
                        'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                        'auction_name': parts[2],
                        'bidder_name': parts[3],
                        'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                        'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                    }
                    bid_history.append(history)
    return bid_history


def write_bid_history(bid_history):
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as file:
        for h in bid_history:
            line = '|'.join([
                str(h['history_id']),
                str(h['auction_id']),
                h['auction_name'],
                h['bidder_name'],
                f"{h['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                h['bid_timestamp']
            ])
            file.write(line + '\n')


def read_trending():
    trending = []
    path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'trending.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
            for line in file:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 6:
                    trend = {
                        'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'item_name': parts[1],
                        'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                        'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                        'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                        'time_period': parts[5]
                    }
                    trending.append(trend)
    return trending


# Routes Implementation

@app.route('/')
def index():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))


@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    auctions = read_auctions()
    trending = read_trending()

    # featured_auctions: top 5 active auctions by soonest end_time (ascending)
    featured_auctions = [a for a in auctions if a['status'] == 'Active']
    featured_auctions.sort(key=lambda x: x['end_time'])
    featured_auctions = featured_auctions[:5]

    # trending_auctions: from trending.txt top 5 by trending_rank time_period 'This Week'
    trending_auctions = [t for t in trending if t['time_period'] == 'This Week']
    trending_auctions.sort(key=lambda x: x['trending_rank'])
    trending_auctions = trending_auctions[:5]

    context_featured = []
    for a in featured_auctions:
        context_featured.append({
            'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
            'item_name': a['item_name'],
            'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
            'end_time': a['end_time'],
            'image_url': a['image_url']
        })

    context_trending = []
    for t in trending_auctions:
        context_trending.append({
            'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
            'item_name': t['item_name'],
            'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
            'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
            'trending_rank': t['trending_rank']
        })

    return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_auctions=context_featured, trending_auctions=context_trending)


@app.route('/catalog')
def auction_catalog():
    auctions = read_auctions()
    categories = read_categories()

    context_auctions = []
    for a in auctions:
        context_auctions.append({
            'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
            'item_name': a['item_name'],
            'description': a['description'],
            'category': a['category'],
            'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
            'end_time': a['end_time'],
            'image_url': a['image_url']
        })

    context_categories = [c['category_name'] for c in categories]

    return render_template('auction_catalog.html', auctions=context_auctions, categories=context_categories)


@app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
def auction_details(auction_id):
    auctions = read_auctions()
    auction = None
    for a in auctions:
        if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            auction = a
            break

    if auction is None:
        return "Auction not found", 404

    bid_history = read_bid_history()
    filtered_bids = []
    for b in bid_history:
        if b['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            filtered_bids.append({
                'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'],
                'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'],
                'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']
            })

    return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=filtered_bids)


@app.route('/place_bid/<int:auction_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def place_bid(auction_id):
    auctions = read_auctions()
    auction = None
    for a in auctions:
        if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            auction = a
            break
    if auction is None:
        return "Auction not found", 404

    submission_response = ''

    if request.method == 'POST':
        bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder_name', '').strip()
        bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid_amount', '').strip()

        # Minimal validation
        if not bidder_name:
            submission_response = 'Bidder name is required.'
        else:
            try:
                bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
                minimum_bid = auction['current_bid']
                if bid_amount <= minimum_bid:
                    submission_response = f'Bid must be greater than current bid ({minimum_bid}).'
                else:
                    from datetime import datetime
                    # Update auctions.txt current_bid
                    auction['current_bid'] = bid_amount
                    write_auctions(auctions)

                    # Add new bid to bids.txt
                    bids = read_bids()
                    new_bid_id = max([b['bid_id'] for b in bids], default=0) + 1
                    new_bid = {
                        'bid_id': new_bid_id,
                        'auction_id': auction_id,
                        'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                        'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                        'bid_timestamp': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
                    }
                    bids.append(new_bid)
                    write_bids(bids)

                    # Add to bid_history.txt
                    bid_history = read_bid_history()
                    new_history_id = max([h['history_id'] for h in bid_history], default=0) + 1
                    new_history = {
                        'history_id': new_history_id,
                        'auction_id': auction_id,
                        'auction_name': auction['item_name'],
                        'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                        'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                        'bid_timestamp': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
                    }
                    bid_history.append(new_history)
                    write_bid_history(bid_history)

                    submission_response = 'Bid placed successfully.'
            except ValueError:
                submission_response = 'Invalid bid amount.'

    context_auction = {
        'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],
        'item_name': auction['item_name'],
        'minimum_bid': auction['current_bid']
    }

    return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=context_auction, submission_response=submission_response)


@app.route('/bid_history')
def bid_history():
    bids = read_bid_history()
    auctions = read_auctions()
    auction_id_to_name = {a['auction_id']: a['item_name'] for a in auctions}

    context_bids = []
    for b in bids:
        context_bids.append({
            'bid_id': b['history_id'] if 'history_id' in b else b['bid_id'],
            'auction_name': b['auction_name'] if 'auction_name' in b else auction_id_to_name.get(b['auction_id'], ''),
            'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'],
            'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'],
            'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']
        })

    context_auctions = []
    for a in auctions:
        context_auctions.append({
            'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
            'item_name': a['item_name']
        })

    return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=context_bids, auctions=context_auctions)


@app.route('/categories')
def auction_categories():
    categories = read_categories()

    # categories context: category_id, category_name, description, item_count
    return render_template('auction_categories.html', categories=categories)


@app.route('/winners')
def winners():
    winners_data = read_winners()

    # filtered_by initially None or empty string
    filtered_by = ''

    winners_context = []
    for w in winners_data:
        winners_context.append({
            'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
            'item_name': w['item_name'],
            'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
            'winning_bid': w['winning_bid']
        })

    return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_context, filtered_by=filtered_by)


@app.route('/trending')
def trending_auctions():
    trending = read_trending()

    # showing all trending auctions (no specific filter for time range from spec)
    context_trending = []
    for t in trending:
        context_trending.append({
            'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
            'item_name': t['item_name'],
            'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
            'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
            'trending_rank': t['trending_rank'],
            'time_period': t['time_period']
        })

    return render_template('trending_auctions.html', trending_auctions=context_trending)


@app.route('/status')
def auction_status():
    auctions = read_auctions()

    # auctions context required: auction_id, item_name, status, time_remaining, current_bid
    # time_remaining can be calculated from end_time but spec does not require exact datetime logic, so show end_time instead as time_remaining for simplicity

    context_auctions = []
    for a in auctions:
        context_auctions.append({
            'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
            'item_name': a['item_name'],
            'status': a['status'],
            'time_remaining': a['end_time'],  # Using end_time string as time_remaining
            'current_bid': a['current_bid']
        })

    return render_template('auction_status.html', auctions=context_auctions)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid_amount', '').strip()          # Minimal validation         if not bidder_name:             submission_response = 'Bidder name is required.'         else:             try:                 bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)                 minimum_bid = auction['current_bid']                 if bid_amount <= minimum_bid:                     submission_response = f'Bid must be greater than current bid ({minimum_bid}).'                 else:                     from datetime import datetime                     # Update auctions.txt current_bid                     auction['current_bid'] = bid_amount                     write_auctions(auctions)                      # Add new bid to bids.txt                     bids = read_bids()                     new_bid_id = max([b['bid_id'] for b in bids], default=0) + 1                     new_bid = {                         'bid_id': new_bid_id,                         'auction_id': auction_id,                         'bidder_name': bidder_name,                         'bid_amount': bid_amount,                         'bid_timestamp': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')                     }                     bids.append(new_bid)                     write_bids(bids)                      # Add to bid_history.txt                     bid_history = read_bid_history()                     new_history_id = max([h['history_id'] for h in bid_history], default=0) + 1                     new_history = {                         'history_id': new_history_id,                         'auction_id': auction_id,                         'auction_name': auction['item_name'],                         'bidder_name': bidder_name,                         'bid_amount': bid_amount,                         'bid_timestamp': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')                     }                     bid_history.append(new_history)                     write_bid_history(bid_history)                      submission_response = 'Bid placed successfully.'             except ValueError:                 submission_response = 'Invalid bid amount.'      context_auction = {         'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],         'item_name': auction['item_name'],         'minimum_bid': auction['current_bid']     }      return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=context_auction, submission_response=submission_response)   @app.route('/bid_history') def bid_history():     bids = read_bid_history()     auctions = read_auctions()     auction_id_to_name = {a['auction_id']: a['item_name'] for a in auctions}      context_bids = []     for b in bids:         context_bids.append({             'bid_id': b['history_id'] if 'history_id' in b else b['bid_id'],             'auction_name': b['auction_name'] if 'auction_name' in b else auction_id_to_name.get(b['auction_id'], ''),             'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'],             'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'],             'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']         })      context_auctions = []     for a in auctions:         context_auctions.append({             'auction_id': a['auction_id'],             'item_name': a['item_name']         })      return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=context_bids, auctions=context_auctions)   @app.route('/categories') def auction_categories():     categories = read_categories()      # categories context: category_id, category_name, description, item_count     return render_template('auction_categories.html', categories=categories)   @app.route('/winners') def winners():     winners_data = read_winners()      # filtered_by initially None or empty string     filtered_by = ''      winners_context = []     for w in winners_data:         winners_context.append({             'auction_id': w['auction_id'],             'item_name': w['item_name'],             'winner_name': w['winner_name'],             'winning_bid': w['winning_bid']         })      return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_context, filtered_by=filtered_by)   @app.route('/trending') def trending_auctions():     trending = read_trending()      # showing all trending auctions (no specific filter for time range from spec)     context_trending = []     for t in trending:         context_trending.append({             'auction_id': t['auction_id'],             'item_name': t['item_name'],             'bid_count': t['bid_count'],             'current_bid': t['current_bid'],             'trending_rank': t['trending_rank'],             'time_period': t['time_period']         })      return render_template('trending_auctions.html', trending_auctions=context_trending)   @app.route('/status') def auction_status():     auctions = read_auctions()      # auctions context required: auction_id, item_name, status, time_remaining, current_bid     # time_remaining can be calculated from end_time but spec does not require exact datetime logic, so show end_time instead as time_remaining for simplicity      context_auctions = []     for a in auctions:         context_auctions.append({             'auction_id': a['auction_id'],             'item_name': a['item_name'],             'status': a['status'],             'time_remaining': a['end_time'],  # Using end_time string as time_remaining             'current_bid': a['current_bid']         })      return render_template('auction_status.html', auctions=context_auctions)   if __name__ == '__main__':     app.run(debug=True, port=5000)
